\index{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}!Mtc\_SessATrsf@{Mtc\_SessATrsf}}
\index{Mtc\_SessATrsf@{Mtc\_SessATrsf}!com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessATrsf()}{Mtc\_SessATrsf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+A\+Trsf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{int}]{i\+Trsf\+Sess }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC session attended transfer. 

If attended transfer successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Acpt

If attended transfer failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Failed, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Term

while receiving attended transfer, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Refered


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to make attended transfer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Trsf\+Sess} & The destination session to which you want to transfer this session.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
If you have a session with user A(indicated by i\+Sess\+Id) and a session with user B(indicated by i\+Trsf\+Sess\+Id), the result of attended transfer is A will have a session with B and all sessions you had with A and B will be terminated.

\index{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}!Mtc\_SessCall@{Mtc\_SessCall}}
\index{Mtc\_SessCall@{Mtc\_SessCall}!com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessCall()}{Mtc\_SessCall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Object}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Video,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Add\+Ext }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Outgoing, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Termed

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Incoming.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Replaced.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Add\+Ext} & Indicate whether this call add extension header.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT, if return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT, should call Mtc\+\_\+\+Lcs\+Get\+Err\+Code 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a7f4b7d2c1efd3e7d6b2358fe2ff9ebc8}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Answer}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_adc0210258db5b6fe566987170ca7c5f4}\label{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_adc0210258db5b6fe566987170ca7c5f4}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+CallX (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Object}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Video,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Send,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Recv }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Outgoing, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Termed

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Incoming.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Replaced.

The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Send} & Indicate whether this call start to send after established. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Recv} & Indicate whether this call start to receive after established.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT.

M\+TC session enable/disable dynamic reset encoder to change video image aspect. The function should be called before \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a7c5d72418cf36e0afed514ae1e37c5f0}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Camera\+Attach}}.

\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em f\+Fixed\+Aspect,if} & $<$ 0 the outgoing video image will be adaptive the capture (camera, always 4\+:3) aspect, if =0 it will use codec settings(always 16\+:9, to be adaptive with the devices), if $>$0 will be with the setting fixed aspect(like 1.\+33, 1.\+77).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

M\+TC session get called U\+RI and display name. Return P-\/\+Called-\/\+Party-\/\+ID header value in S\+IP invite message, other return TO header value. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to get. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ppc\+Disp\+Name} & The display name of called party. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The U\+RI of called party.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The caller must copy out parameter, then use.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
The called party information get by this function is actually from P-\/\+Called-\/\+Party-\/\+ID or TO header in S\+IP message. So the true identity of called user is not asserted by local U\+RI especially in the case of S\+IP gateway receiving an incoming call. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a811091e350e0201159629be8ef1a5d82}\label{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a811091e350e0201159629be8ef1a5d82}}

{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
The peer information get by this function is actually from F\+R\+O\+M/\+TO header in S\+IP message. So the true identity of peer user is not asserted by server.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessHold()}{Mtc\_SessHold()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Hold (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i\+Sess\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC session hold. 

If sending session hold successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Hold\+Ok

If sending session hold failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Hold\+Failed

While receiving session held, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Held.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to hold.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessPickUp()}{Mtc\_SessPickUp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Pick\+Up (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{String}]{pc\+Replace\+Info,  }\item[{Object}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Video }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC Pick\+Up, establishing session call with video or audio by replacing specific call. 

If the new session call was accept by callee, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking.

If the new session call was reject by callee or no answer, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Termed.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Replace\+Info} & The replace information used to locate replaced call. The format must comply with R\+F\+C3891, like \textquotesingle{}\href{mailto:425928@phone.example.org}{\texttt{ 425928@phone.\+example.\+org}};to-\/tag=7743;from-\/tag=6472\textquotesingle{}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a4ac86fce5481f4b6516bb17ff982a3ff}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Pick\+UpX}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a4ac86fce5481f4b6516bb17ff982a3ff}\label{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a4ac86fce5481f4b6516bb17ff982a3ff}}

\index{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}!Mtc\_SessRadioCall@{Mtc\_SessRadioCall}}
\index{Mtc\_SessRadioCall@{Mtc\_SessRadioCall}!com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessRadioCall()}{Mtc\_SessRadioCall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Radio\+Call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Object}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Video,  }\item[{int}]{i\+Serv\+Info\+Type,  }\item[{int}]{i\+Term\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Outgoing, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Talking

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Alerted, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Termed

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Incoming.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Replaced.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Serv\+Info\+Type} & Indicate type of server info, Mtc\+Call\+Constants\+::\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+P2P. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Term\+Type} & Indicate type of the seat terminal, Mtc\+Call\+Constants\+::\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+WN.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a7f4b7d2c1efd3e7d6b2358fe2ff9ebc8}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Answer}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a1ada8de57929c99bbd92fb6690541add}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a00a652166ff626ed5d4de3d796c83bd5}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Unhold (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i\+Sess\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC session unhold. 

If sending session unhold successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Un\+Hold\+Ok

If sending session hold failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Un\+Hold\+Failed

While receiving session unheld, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Un\+Held.

\index{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}!Mtc\_SessUpdate@{Mtc\_SessUpdate}}
\index{Mtc\_SessUpdate@{Mtc\_SessUpdate}!com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessUpdate()}{Mtc\_SessUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{boolean}]{b\+Video }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC session send a media update request to peer. The update in this function means open a new media stream or close an already exist media stream. 

If sending update successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Audio\+Ok, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Rmv\+Audio\+Ok, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Video\+Ok, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Rmv\+Video\+Ok

If sending update failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Audio\+Failed, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Rmv\+Audio\+Failed, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Video\+Failed, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Rmv\+Video\+Failed

While receiving update, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Audio\+Req, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Add\+Video\+Req.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to update its media. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether you want to have a audio stream after update. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether you want to have a video stream after update.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
If the update request is accepted by peer, an indication will arise through the callback function which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Mdfy\+Acpt.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a02b2ac43e236c795b8b937a8a23564c6}{Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Update\+Rsp}}, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Mdfy\+Acpt 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a02b2ac43e236c795b8b937a8a23564c6}\label{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_call_a02b2ac43e236c795b8b937a8a23564c6}}

M\+TC session response a media update request from peer. The update in this function means open a new media stream or close an already exist media stream. 

If sending negotiate successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Mdfyed

\index{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}!Mtc\_SessUTrsf@{Mtc\_SessUTrsf}}
\index{Mtc\_SessUTrsf@{Mtc\_SessUTrsf}!com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall@{com.juphoon.cmcc.app.lemon.MtcCall}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessUTrsf()}{Mtc\_SessUTrsf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Call.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+U\+Trsf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{String}]{pc\+Uri }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



M\+TC session unattended transfer. 

If unattended transfer successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Acpt

If unattended transfer failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Failed, mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Trsf\+Term

while receiving unattended transfer, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by mtc\+Call\+Cb\+Refered


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to make unattended transfer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to transfer this session.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
After this operation, the session will be terminated by server.
